## ダイエット・筋トレ Core-1. Exercise- and dietary pattern-based lifestyle interventions and neurocognitive function in adults: a Bayesian multilevel network and dose-response meta-analysis.

- Candidate bucket: Core
- 事前スコア: 16
- PMID: 42334484
- DOI: 10.1007/s00415-026-13918-7
- Journal: Journal of neurology
- PubDate: 2026-06-23
- PublicationType: Journal Article; Network Meta-Analysis; Systematic Review; Review
- PubMed: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42334484/
- OpenAlex cited_by_count: 0

Abstract:
OBJECTIVE: To systematically review the effects of lifestyle interventions focused on exercise and dietary patterns on neurocognitive function in adults, and to examine their relative effects and dose-response relationships.
METHODS: PubMed, Embase, Web of Science, and the Cochrane Library were searched from database inception to March 20, 2026. A total of 23 randomized controlled trials (RCTs) involving 12,286 participants were included. Bayesian multilevel pairwise, network, and dose-response meta-analyses were conducted to evaluate overall cognition, memory, and executive function. RoB 2 and CINeMA were used to assess the credibility of the evidence.
RESULTS: Combined interventions yielded small, but statistically significant cognitive benefits (overall cognition: SMD = 0.18; memory: SMD = 0.10; executive function: SMD = 0.09). These benefits were driven primarily by differences between the combined intervention and control or usual care, as well as exercise alone; compared with diet alone, the combined intervention still showed a small advantage for executive function. Network meta-analysis suggested that AE_MIND and AE_RT_MED were more beneficial for overall cognition, AE_RT_MIND and AE_RT_MED for memory, and AE_RT_CR and AE_MIND for executive function. Exploratory dose-response analyses suggested possible curvature in some spline-based models; however, comparison with simpler monotonic specifications did not provide robust evidence for a clinically interpretable non-linear or monotonic dose-response relationship.
CONCLUSION: Combined lifestyle interventions may produce statistically significant but modest improvements in cognitive function in adults, with benefits varying across cognitive domains. However, current evidence remains insufficient to support a standardized precision prescription, and high-quality RCTs with long-term follow-up are needed to determine the optimal combinations and dosages.

## ダイエット・筋トレ Core-2. Inhaled nitric oxide in fibrotic and advanced interstitial lung disease: A systematic review and meta-analysis of randomized controlled trials.

- Candidate bucket: Core
- 事前スコア: 16
- PMID: 42329957
- DOI: 10.1371/journal.pone.0351862
- Journal: PloS one
- PubDate: 2026
- PublicationType: Journal Article; Systematic Review; Meta-Analysis
- PubMed: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42329957/
- OA URL: https://doi.org/10.1371/journal.pone.0351862
- OpenAlex cited_by_count: 0

Abstract:
PURPOSE: Interstitial lung disease (ILD) can lead to pulmonary hypertension (PH), contributing to reduced exercise capacity in patients with ILD. Inhaled nitric oxide (iNO) reduces pulmonary artery pressure and pulmonary vascular resistance and may improve exercise capacity in this population; however, the available evidence remains limited. Therefore, we conducted a systematic review and meta-analysis to compare the efficacy and safety of iNO versus placebo in patients with ILD.
METHODS: We systematically searched PubMed, Embase, Cochrane databases, and ClinicalTrials.gov for randomized controlled trials (RCTs) comparing iNO with placebo in patients with ILD. The primary endpoint was 6-minute walk distance (6MWD). Secondary endpoint was moderate-to-vigorous physical activity (MVPA). Safety endpoint was any adverse events. Continuous endpoints were reported using mean differences (MDs) or standardized mean differences (SMDs), and binary endpoints were reported using risk ratios (RRs), all with 95% confidence intervals (CIs).
RESULTS: Four RCTs, including one crossover trial, enrolling 274 patients were analyzed. Of these, 172 received iNO. The median follow-up period was 12 weeks. In the pooled analyses, iNO likely results in little to no difference in 6MWD compared with placebo (MD 1.83m; 95% CI -12.98 to 16.64; p = 0.81), and may result in little to no difference in any adverse events (RR 1.12; 95% CI 0.97 to 1.30; p = 0.12) and MVPA (SMD 0.32; 95% CI -0.93 to 1.56; p = 0.39).
CONCLUSION: INO did not demonstrate improvements in 6MWD or MVPA. These findings do not support routine use of iNO in this population.

## ダイエット・筋トレ Core-3. The effect of Pemafibrate on glucose metabolism and FGF21: a systematic review and meta-analysisa of randomized controlled trials.

- Candidate bucket: Core
- 事前スコア: 16
- PMID: 42329272
- DOI: 10.1007/s00228-026-04113-8
- Journal: European journal of clinical pharmacology
- PubDate: 2026-06-22
- PublicationType: Journal Article; Systematic Review; Meta-Analysis; Review
- PubMed: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42329272/
- OpenAlex cited_by_count: 0

Abstract:
BACKGROUND: Pemafibrate, a selective peroxisome proliferator-activated receptor alpha (PPARα) modulator, has shown potential in improving metabolic parameters. However, its effects on key metabolic biomarkers and fibroblast growth factor 21 (FGF21), have not been fully elucidated. To evaluate the effects of Pemafibrate on fasting blood glucose (FBG), insulin, HbA1c, HOMA-IR, and FGF21 through a systematic review and meta-analysis of randomized controlled trials (RCTs).
METHODS: A comprehensive literature search was conducted in PubMed, Web of Science, SCOPUS, and Embase databases from their inception until November 2025. RCTs assessing the effects of Pemafibrate on the selected metabolic biomarkers were included and the weighted mean differences (WMD) for each outcome were calculated using a random-effects model.
RESULTS: A total of 14 RCTs with 4084 participants were included in the present meta-analysis. Pemafibrate significantly reduced FBG (11 studies, 3273 patients, WMD = -0.47 mmol/L, 95% CI: -0.70 to -0.24), insulin levels (7 studies, 2102 patients, WMD = -30.72 pmol/L, 95% CI: -42.08 to -19.36), and HOMA-IR (8 studies, 2381 patients, WMD = -1.60, 95% CI: -2.27 to -0.93). Additionally, FGF21 levels were significantly increased (7 studies, 2178 patients, WMD = 3.30 pg/mL, 95% CI: 2.57 to 4.04). The effect on HbA1c was marginally non-significant (10 studies, 3065 patients, WMD = 0.02%, 95% CI: 0.00 to 0.05). Subgroup analysis revealed that lower duration of Pemafibrate intake were associated with significant improvements in FBG, while higher doses (> 0.2 mg/day) had more pronounced effects on FGF21 and glucoe metabolism. Meta-regression indicated that treatment duration was positively correlated with reductions in insulin levels. The overall GRADE quality assessment was rated as very good, supporting a moderate-to-high level of confidence.
CONCLUSIONS: Pemafibrate significantly improves glucose metabolism, insulin sensitivity, and increases FGF21 levels, making it a promising therapeutic option for patients with metabolic disorders.

## ダイエット・筋トレ Core-4. Effects of Bilateral Robotic Arm Training in Stroke Patients: A Systematic Review and Meta-Analysis.

- Candidate bucket: Core
- 事前スコア: 16
- PMID: 42346832
- DOI: 10.3390/medsci14020293
- Journal: Medical sciences (Basel, Switzerland)
- PubDate: 2026-06-05
- PublicationType: Journal Article; Systematic Review; Meta-Analysis; Review
- PubMed: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42346832/
- OA URL: https://doi.org/10.3390/medsci14020293
- OpenAlex cited_by_count: 0

Abstract:
: Bilateral robotic arm training (BRT) may enhance poststroke motor recovery by reducing interhemispheric inhibition and promoting bilateral motor network engagement. However, previous reviews have often pooled bilateral and unilateral robotic approaches, potentially masking differential effects. This systematic review and meta-analysis compared the effects of BRT with those of unilateral robotic training (URT) and conventional rehabilitation on upper-limb motor function after stroke. : Randomized controlled trials were identified through systematic searches of major electronic databases and trial registries in accordance with PRISMA guidelines. The risk of bias was assessed via the Cochrane Risk of Bias 2 tool. Random effects meta-analyses were performed using standardized mean differences (SMDs). Predefined subgroup and sensitivity analyses were used to examine the influence of participant characteristics, training dose, intervention duration, and robotic device type. : Fourteen randomized controlled trials involving 440 participants were included. Overall, compared with control interventions, BRT did not significantly improve upper-limb motor function, as measured using the Fugl-Meyer Assessment for Upper Extremity (SMD = 0.18, 95% CI -0.01-0.36). Significant effects were observed in participants younger than 60 years, with training doses > 15 h, intervention durations > 4 weeks, and use of Bi-Manu-Track systems. : BRT did not demonstrate a significant overall advantage over URT or conventional rehabilitation. However, subgroup analyses suggest that treatment effects may vary according to patient characteristics, training dose, duration of the intervention, and device type.

## ダイエット・筋トレ Core-5. Efficacy of non-pharmacological interventions for knee osteoarthritis in the elderly: A systematic review and meta-analysis.

- Candidate bucket: Core
- 事前スコア: 15
- PMID: 42332451
- DOI: 10.1097/MD.0000000000048984
- Journal: Medicine
- PubDate: 2026-06-19
- PublicationType: Journal Article; Systematic Review; Meta-Analysis
- PubMed: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42332451/
- OA URL: https://doi.org/10.1097/md.0000000000048984
- OpenAlex cited_by_count: 0

Abstract:
BACKGROUND: Knee osteoarthritis (KOA) is highly prevalent in the elderly. Non-pharmacological treatments are recommended as first-line management, but high-quality evidence synthesis is lacking.
METHODS: We conducted a systematic review and meta-analysis following Preferred Reporting Items for Systematic Reviews and Meta-Analyses 2020 guidelines. Databases were searched from January 2002 to July 2025. Two reviewers independently screened literature, extracted data, and assessed risk of bias using Cochrane Risk of Bias 2.0. Meta-analysis was performed using a random-effects model.
RESULTS: A total of 13 randomized controlled trials were included in this meta-analysis. Exercise therapy significantly relieved pain and improved physical function in elderly patients with KOA (standardized mean difference [SMD] = -0.66, 95% confidence interval (CI): -1.25 to -0.06, I2 = 80%) (after sensitivity analysis). TCM non-pharmacological therapies also yielded significant beneficial effects (SMD = -0.21, 95% CI: -0.54 to 0.12, I2 = 72%), whereas physical therapy modalities showed no statistically significant difference (SMD = -0.16, 95% CI: -0.43 to 0.10, I2 = 65%). High heterogeneity was mainly attributed to diverse outcome measurement scales and intervention intensity, duration, and protocols.
CONCLUSION: Non-pharmacological interventions effectively relieve pain and improve function in elderly KOA patients. Exercise therapy is the most consistent and reliable intervention.

## ダイエット・筋トレ Core-6. Proximal femoral bionic nail (PFBN) versus InterTAN nail for intertrochanteric femoral fractures in elderly patients: a systematic review and meta-analysis.

Abstract:

CONCLUSION: Based on the limited evidence from current non-randomized studies, PFBN exhibits potential benefits in shortening hospital duration and reducing the risk of internal fixation-related complications among elderly patients with intertrochanteric femoral fractures. Meanwhile, this implant yields equivalent effects to the InterTAN nail with regard to functional recovery. ## ダイエット・筋トレ Core-7. Thrombosis-Associated Risk Factors in Pediatrics and Adults Treated with Asparaginase-Containing Chemotherapy for ALL: A Systematic Review and Meta-Analysis.

- Candidate bucket: Core

- PMID: 42346268
- DOI: 10.3390/curroncol33060368
- Journal: Current oncology (Toronto, Ont.)
- PubDate: 2026-06-18
- PublicationType: Journal Article; Systematic Review; Meta-Analysis; Review

- OpenAlex cited_by_count: 0

Abstract:
: Thromboembolism is a serious complication in acute lymphoblastic leukemia (ALL). This systematic review and meta-analysis evaluated thrombosis incidence and risk factors across populations receiving asparaginase-based therapy. : From 214 studies (1994-2026), 58 met inclusion criteria, totaling 23,655 adult, pediatric, and mixed-population patients. Searches included Ovid MEDLINE, Embase, Cochrane CENTRAL, PubMed Central, and Google Scholar. Eligible studies were observational cohorts or clinical trials reporting thrombosis in ALL patients treated with asparaginase. Adults and older children had higher risk, and pediatric patients with overweight/obesity, mediastinal mass, or non-O blood type were particularly vulnerable. Thromboprophylaxis is advised for high-risk groups. This review was not registered and received no external funding.

## ダイエット・筋トレ Core-8. Compliance With Physical Activity, Sedentary Behaviour and Sleep Recommendations in Children Aged 5-13 Years: A Systematic Review and Meta-Analysis Across 15 Countries.

- Candidate bucket: Core
- 事前スコア: 14
- PMID: 42338101
- DOI: 10.1111/cch.70307
- Journal: Child: care, health and development
- PubDate: 2026-07-01
- PublicationType: Journal Article; Systematic Review; Meta-Analysis; Review
- PubMed: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42338101/
- OpenAlex cited_by_count: 0

Abstract:
BACKGROUND: Several regions have published 24-h Movement Guidelines recommending durations of moderate-to-vigorous physical activity (MVPA), recreational screen time (ST) and sleep. This study aimed to investigate the global prevalence of school-aged children meeting the individual and combined recommendations of the 24-h Movement Guidelines.
METHOD: Six databases were initially searched from 2016 to 2025 and further updated in May 2026. This review included studies reporting adherence rates to the 24-h Movement Guidelines, including none, individual (MVPA, ST, sleep), combined (MVPA&ST, MVPA&sleep, ST&sleep) and all three guidelines among children aged 5-13 years. A random-effects model was used to pool prevalence rates across studies.
RESULT: Twenty-nine studies involving 83 396 school-aged children were included in the analysis, and only 10.2% met all three 24-h Movement Guidelines. Among individual and combined guidelines, adherence was the lowest for the MVPA&ST guideline (6.0%), followed by MVPA (7.9%), all three guidelines (10.2%) and MVPA&sleep (10.2%) guideline.
CONCLUSION: Overall adherence to the 24-h Movement Guidelines among school-aged children is low, with the lower compliance for MVPA&ST guideline and MVPA guideline. Targeted interventions to increase MVPA may improve overall compliance.

## ダイエット・筋トレ Core-9. Investigating the Effect of Blood Groups on the Risk of Musculoskeletal Injuries: A Systematic Review.

- Candidate bucket: Core
- 事前スコア: 13
- PMID: 42348571
- DOI: 10.1097/JSM.0000000000001463
- Journal: Clinical journal of sport medicine : official journal of the Canadian Academy of Sport Medicine
- PubDate: 2026-07-01
- PublicationType: Journal Article; Systematic Review
- PubMed: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42348571/
- OpenAlex cited_by_count: 0

Abstract:
OBJECTIVE: Human blood groups classically are described: A, B, AB, and O, and the presence or absence of the Rh antigen on them plays an important role in determining these groups. Previous studies have examined the relationship between blood groups and metabolic diseases. However, no study has yet investigated the relationship between blood groups and musculoskeletal injuries, and this issue has not been fully clarified. This systematic review investigates the association between blood groups and the risk of musculoskeletal injuries.
DATA SOURCES: This study was conducted according to the guidelines Preferred Reporting Items for Systematic Reviews and Meta-Analyses. PubMed and Web of Science databases were searched and included in the present systematic review. The quality assessment tool for observational and cross-sectional cohort studies checked the articles' quality.
MAIN RESULTS: A total of 12 cross-sectional studies were included in the present systematic review. The results showed that the amount of injury in people with different blood groups is different. For example, common fractures and osteoporosis were more in people with blood group A, and tendon injury was in people with blood group O.
CONCLUSIONS: People with certain blood groups may be more prone to some musculoskeletal injuries.

## ダイエット・筋トレ Core-10. Workplace interventions for chronic musculoskeletal disorders: a systematic review.

- Candidate bucket: Core
- 事前スコア: 13
- PMID: 42331580
- DOI: 10.1136/bmjopen-2025-115276
- Journal: BMJ open
- PubDate: 2026-06-22
- PublicationType: Journal Article; Systematic Review
- PubMed: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42331580/
- OA URL: https://doi.org/10.1136/bmjopen-2025-115276
- OpenAlex cited_by_count: 0

Abstract:
OBJECTIVES: To provide an updated systematic review of the effectiveness of workplace interventions for chronic musculoskeletal disorders, identify key intervention components and assess their impact on health and work-related outcomes.
DESIGN: Systematic review of randomised controlled trials.
DATA SOURCES: MEDLINE, EMBASE, CINAHL, PsycINFO, Scopus and Web of Science were searched for studies published between 2018 and 2024. Grey literature sources were also consulted.
ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA: Randomised controlled trials and cluster-randomised trials evaluating workplace interventions targeting adults with chronic musculoskeletal disorders were included. Outcomes of interest included pain, functional outcomes, quality of life and work-related outcomes (eg, work ability, productivity, presenteeism and absenteeism).
DATA EXTRACTION AND SYNTHESIS: Two reviewers independently screened studies, extracted data and assessed risk of bias using the Cochrane Risk of Bias 2 tool. Due to heterogeneity, only a narrative synthesis was conducted.
RESULTS: 23 studies involving 2456 participants were included and classified into physical exercise, ergonomic and multicomponent interventions. Physical exercise interventions consistently improved pain and functional outcomes. Digital delivery of exercise interventions demonstrated comparable effectiveness to face-to-face or workplace-based approaches. Multicomponent interventions, combining exercise with ergonomic strategies, demonstrated the most consistent benefits across outcomes. Evidence for work-related outcomes was limited and inconsistent, and quality of life was assessed in only a small number of studies.
CONCLUSIONS: Workplace interventions, particularly multicomponent approaches combining exercise, ergonomics and education, can be effective in improving health outcomes in chronic musculoskeletal disorders. However, evidence on work-related outcomes remains limited and inconsistent.
PROSPERO REGISTRATION NUMBER: CRD420261289218.

## ダイエット・筋トレ Reserve-1. Long-Term Safety and Renal Outcomes of Semaglutide in Non-Diabetic Obesity with Chronic Kidney Disease or Hypertension: A Systematic Review and Meta-Analysis.

- Candidate bucket: Reserve
- 事前スコア: 13
- PMID: 42340790
- DOI: 10.7417/CT.2026.2083
- Journal: La Clinica terapeutica
- PubDate: 2026
- PublicationType: Journal Article; Systematic Review
- PubMed: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42340790/
- OpenAlex cited_by_count: 0

Abstract:
BACKGROUND: Semaglutide, a GLP-1 receptor agonist, has demonstrated metabolic and renal benefits in diabetic populations. However, its efficacy and safety in non-diabetic individuals with obesity and chronic kidney disease (CKD) remain largely unstudied. Given the high cardiometabolic risk in this group and limited therapeutic options, evaluating semaglutide's role is crucial.
OBJECTIVE: To assess the effects of semaglutide on body mass index (BMI), blood pressure, renal function (eGFR), and albuminuria in non-diabetic patients with obesity and CKD or hypertension.
METHODS: This systematic review and meta-analysis was conducted in accordance with PRISMA guidelines. A total of 580 studies were screened; 3 eligible studies (n=430 participants) were included. Data were extracted from a randomized controlled trial, a real-world observational dialysis study, and a large post hoc trial analysis. Fixed-effect meta-analysis models were applied to estimate pooled effects on BMI, systolic blood pressure (SBP), and renal outcomes.
RESULTS: Semaglutide treatment significantly reduced BMI (mean reduction: Tuttle 18.3%, Apperloo 11.8%, Vanek 1.5%; P = 0.001), and improved hypertension control (SBP <130 mmHg: Apperloo 20.6%, Vanek 12.5%, Tuttle 17.6%; P < 0.02). Renal function also improved, with eGFR >30 ml/min/1.73m² increasing from baseline in all studies (Apperloo 65.8%, Vanek 4.83%, Tuttle 36.4%; P < 0.001). No publication bias was detected.
CONCLUSIONS: Semaglutide is effective and well-tolerated in non-diabetic patients with obesity and CKD, resulting in significant weight loss, better blood pressure control, and improved renal parameters. These findings support its expanded use in non-diabetic CKD populations, including dialysis-dependent individuals.

## ダイエット・筋トレ Reserve-4. Post-diagnosis physical activity in relation to mortality among prostate cancer survivors: a systematic review and meta-analysis.

- Candidate bucket: Reserve
- 事前スコア: 12
- PMID: 42348026
- DOI: 10.1007/s10552-026-02197-2
- Journal: Cancer causes & control : CCC
- PubDate: 2026-06-25
- PublicationType: Systematic Review; Journal Article; Meta-Analysis
- PubMed: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42348026/
- OpenAlex cited_by_count: 0

Abstract:
BACKGROUND: Physical activity after cancer diagnosis may reduce mortality. However, systematic evidence for this association for men living with prostate cancer remains limited.
METHODS: We searched PubMed, Embase, and CINAHL data bases from start to June 2025. Random-effects meta-analyses estimated summary hazard ratios (HRs) and 95% confidence intervals (CI) for all-cause mortality and prostate-cancer-specific mortality to assess the association between post-diagnosis physical activity, measured in metabolic equivalents of task-hours per week (MET-hr/week), and mortality among prostate cancer survivors.
RESULTS: We included ten studies with more than 50,144 participants (one study did not report the number of prostate cancer cases included in the meta-analysis) and 28,044 deaths. Higher levels of post-diagnosis physical activity (≥ 7.5 MET-hr/week) were associated with lower all-cause mortality (HR = 0.69; 95% CI: 0.62-0.77), compared to lower levels (< 7.5 MET-hr/week). Meta-analysis of five studies showed an inverse association between post-diagnosis physical activity and prostate cancer-specific mortality (HR = 0.77; 95% CI: 0.66-0.89). Meta-analysis of four studies showed that moderate-to-vigorous physical activity was inversely associated with mortality (HR = 0.62; 95% CI: 0.51-0.74).
CONCLUSION: Higher post-diagnosis physical activity, including activity at higher intensities, was associated with lower all-cause and prostate cancer-specific mortality among men living with prostate cancer. Our findings suggest that physical activity may complement cancer care for prostate cancer patients.

## ダイエット・筋トレ Reserve-5. Comparative efficacy of various exercise types and doses for anxiety in older adults: A network and dose-response meta-analysis.

- Candidate bucket: Reserve
- 事前スコア: 11
- PMID: 42337443
- DOI: 10.1186/s12877-026-07869-x
- Journal: BMC geriatrics
- PubDate: 2026-06-23
- PublicationType: Journal Article; Systematic Review
- PubMed: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42337443/
- OA URL: https://doi.org/10.1186/s12877-026-07869-x
- OpenAlex cited_by_count: 0

Abstract:
BACKGROUND: Anxiety significantly impacts quality of life among older adults, particularly those with chronic conditions. Exercise has been established as an effective non-pharmacological intervention for anxiety, while the optimal type and dosage of exercise remain unclear. This study aimed to determine which exercise modality yields the largest efficacy for reducing anxiety and to model the optimal METs-min/week dose for anxiety reduction.
METHODS: This systematic review and network meta-analysis searched PubMed, Web of Science, Embase, Medline, and Cochrane databases from database inception to 15 January 2025. We included randomized controlled trials (RCTs) investigating exercise interventions among older adults (≥ 60 years) and extracted data from dose metrics (METs-min/week), treatment regimens, intensity, and study duration.

CONCLUSION: Our findings indicate that Tai Chi is the most effective exercise for alleviating anxiety in older adults. In contrast, MIX showed no significant effects.

BACKGROUND: Platelet-rich plasma (PRP) is widely used as an intra-articular treatment for knee osteoarthritis (KOA), but whether combining PRP with hyaluronic acid (HA), mesenchymal stem cells (MSCs), or ozone (O) provides additional clinical benefit remains unclear. We conducted a systematic review and network meta-analysis (NMA) to compare the efficacy of PRP monotherapy with these three PRP-based combination strategies.
METHODS: Twelve electronic databases were searched from inception to April 2026 for randomized controlled trials (RCTs) that compared intra-articular PRP alone with PRP combined with HA, MSCs, or O in adults with KOA. Two reviewers independently performed study selection, data extraction, and risk of bias assessment using the Cochrane RoB 2 tool. The primary outcomes were changes in WOMAC total score and VAS pain score. A random-effects NMA was conducted within a frequentist framework in Stata 17.0. Treatment rankings were calculated using surface under the cumulative ranking curve (SUCRA) values.
RESULTS: Eighteen RCTs involving 1,376 participants met the inclusion criteria. The evidence network was star-shaped, with PRP alone serving as the sole common comparator. For WOMAC function, PRP + HA was the only combination that demonstrated a statistically significant improvement over PRP alone (MD = - 6.16, 95% CI - 9.71 to - 2.61, P < 0.001). Differences were not significant for PRP + O (MD = - 9.65, 95% CI - 20.33 to 1.03) or PRP + MSC (MD = - 0.80, 95% CI - 12.85 to 11.25). For VAS pain, PRP + HA again showed superior pain relief (MD = - 1.01, 95% CI - 1.57 to - 0.44, P < 0.001). PRP + MSC (MD = - 0.77, 95% CI - 1.92 to 0.38) and PRP + O (MD = - 0.15, 95% CI - 1.87 to 1.57) did not differ significantly from PRP alone. SUCRA values ranked PRP + HA highest for VAS pain and second for WOMAC function. No significant publication bias was detected.
CONCLUSIONS: Among PRP-based combination therapies for KOA, the addition of HA to PRP is supported by the most consistent evidence for improving pain and function. Current data are insufficient to conclude that adding MSCs or O provides any additional benefit. Standardized, large-scale RCTs with longer follow-up are needed to clarify the role of these emerging combinations.

Abstract:

METHODS: We searched five major databases (PubMed, Web of Science, EBSCO, Cochrane, and Scopus) for randomized controlled trials up to March 2025. Studies assessing TCE in patients with PD were included. Data were pooled using the standardized mean difference (SMD) and 95% confidence interval (CI).

TCE demonstrated significant overall improvements in cognition (SMD = 0.87, 95% CI [0.56, 1.19]), sleep quality (SMD, -0.88, 95% CI [-1.41, -0.34]), and QoL (SMD, -0.48, 95% CI [-0.66, -0.29]). Benefits were also more pronounced in patients with a disease duration of 5 years or more.
CONCLUSION: TCE may be beneficial for improving cognition, sleep quality, and QoL in patients with PD. Subgroup findings further suggest that intervention type, duration, and weekly exercise volume may be associated with differential outcomes.

## ダイエット・筋トレ Reserve-9. Associations of the inflammasome-dependent cytokine IL-18 with risk of coronary heart disease.

- Candidate bucket: Reserve
- 事前スコア: 8
- PMID: 42334366
- DOI: 10.1093/cvr/cvag135
- Journal: Cardiovascular research
- PubDate: 2026-06-23
- PublicationType: Journal Article
- PubMed: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42334366/
- OpenAlex cited_by_count: 0

Abstract:
AIMS: Inflammasome activation has emerged as a promising therapeutic target to reduce residual cardiovascular risk in patients on guideline lipid-lowering therapy. IL-1β and IL-6 have been intensively studied, whereas the role of the inflammasome-related cytokine IL-18 has gained less attention. Here we aimed to assess the associations of IL-18 with risk of coronary events and severity of atherosclerosis.
METHODS AND RESULTS: The study included 4,742 participants participating in a prospective Swedish Malmö Diet and Cancer (MDC) cohort study, 54,219 general population participants in the UK Biobank, and 1,500 participants with type 2 diabetes and/or known cardiovascular disease in the European multicenter SUMMIT VIP imaging study. Plasma levels of IL-18 were analyzed using proximity extension assay and atherosclerosis by carotid ultrasound. The incidence of MI and CV death was registered during a 23-year follow-up for MDC cohort and for a 15-year follow-up for the UK Biobank cohort.There were 617 cases of MI and 644 CV deaths in the MDC cohort and 2,454 cases of MI and 1,537 CV deaths in the UK Biobank cohort. Elevated IL-18 was associated with an increased risk of MI and CV death independent of hsCRP and IL-6 in both cohorts. - PMID: 42336782

- PubDate: 2026-06-23

- PubMed: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42336782/

- OpenAlex cited_by_count: 0

Abstract:
OBJECTIVES: This qualitative systematic review aimed to describe the experiences and perspectives of loneliness and social isolation among informal caregivers of people with chronic kidney disease (CKD).
METHODS: Terms for caregivers, qualitative research, loneliness and social isolation and CKD were entered into MEDLINE, Embase, CINAHL and PsycINFO and searched from inception to May 2025. Qualitative studies that described social isolation and loneliness among caregivers of people with CKD were included in this review. Study characteristics were extracted into Microsoft Excel. Qualitative data from each study were imported into HyperRESEARCH and analysed using thematic synthesis.
RESULTS: We included 19 articles involving 598 caregivers of people with CKD from 28 countries. Four major themes with subthemes were identified: confined by the patient's needs (social withdrawal due to unrelenting demands, separated from communities due to treatment, torn between work and caregiving responsibilities, foregoing social outings with family and friends, restricted by patient's diet, feeling protective against infection risk); limited care assistance exacerbating isolation (inadequate familial support, absence of respite care, lacking accessible guidance from health professionals); disrupting relationships and social roles (sacrificing social needs and identity, family conflicts worsening isolation, withdrawing to avoid stigma and ridicule, grappling with hopelessness, reluctance to share struggles); and coping with support resources (connecting with other families, seeking assistance from support services, finding support through faith).
CONCLUSIONS: Caregivers of people with CKD experience restricted social participation and loss of social roles and identity, which can exacerbate feelings of loneliness and social isolation. Support services are needed to prevent and address social isolation and loneliness in CKD caregivers.

## ダイエット・筋トレ Reserve-15. Effects of (Ashwagandha) Supplementation on Exercise Performance: A Systematic Review and Three-Level Meta-Analysis.

- 事前スコア: 7
- PMID: 42356302
- DOI: 10.3390/nu18121915
- Journal: Nutrients
- PubDate: 2026-06-12
- PublicationType: Journal Article; Review
- PubMed: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42356302/
- OA URL: https://doi.org/10.3390/nu18121915
- OpenAlex cited_by_count: 0

Abstract:
BACKGROUND/OBJECTIVES: Evidence for herbal ergogenic aids remains uncertain, and ashwagandha trials span heterogeneous performance domains. This review evaluated oral supplementation on exercise performance and explored participant-, outcome-, formulation-, and supplementation-related moderators.
METHODS: PubMed, Web of Science, Cochrane Library, Embase, and SPORTDiscus-EBSCO were searched from inception to 1 April 2026. Eligible randomized controlled trials compared oral ashwagandha with placebo or control conditions and reported objective exercise-performance outcomes. Dependent effects were synthesized using restricted-maximum-likelihood three-level random-effects models; 95% prediction intervals, GRADE certainty ratings, subgroup analyses, and dose/duration meta-regressions were reported.

Dose analyses were hypothesis-generating; 500-600 mg/day was the most evidence-supported extract-dose range.
CONCLUSIONS: Oral ashwagandha may improve selected exercise-performance outcomes, particularly aerobic endurance, but benefits are not uniform across contexts. Future trials should be preregistered, adequately powered, double-blind, formulation-standardized, sex-stratified, and include rigorous blinding checks, mechanistic endpoints, adverse-event monitoring, and sport-specific performance tests.

## ダイエット・筋トレ Reserve-16. Semaglutide and major adverse cardiovascular events in patients with and without DM: A systematic review and meta-analysis.

- Candidate bucket: Reserve
- 事前スコア: 7

- DOI: 10.3892/br.2026.2165

- PubDate: 2026-08-01

- PubMed: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42339050/
- OpenAlex cited_by_count: 0

Abstract:
Semaglutide, a once-weekly glucagon-like peptide-1 receptor agonist (GLP-1 RA), has been associated with cardiovascular benefits, whereas the consistency of its effect across various clinical settings, as well as its safety-economic profile, remains uncertain. MEDLINE, Embase, Cochrane Central Register of Controlled Trials (CENTRAL), Web of Science, ClinicalTrials.gov and WHO International Clinical Trials Registry Platform were searched up to January 2025 and identified 11 randomized controlled trials (12 comparisons; 25,067 participants) comparing semaglutide with placebo or active control. Using a DerSimonian-Laird random-effects model, semaglutide reduced major adverse cardiovascular events by 32% [pooled odds ratio (OR)=0.68; 95%; confidence interval 0.52-0.91; 95% prediction interval 0.44-1.04]. Point estimates remained unchanged after censoring all STEP obesity trials (OR=0.70) or both heart-failure trials (OR=0.66), indicating a negligible institution-level effect. Mixed-effects meta-regression analysis revealed greater benefit with lower body weight, LDL- and total cholesterol levels, and lesser benefit with higher age, HbA1c and blood pressure (all P<0.01). A total of seven out of 11 trials enrolled ≥75% White patients, none of whom were from low-income countries, limiting generalizability. Besides, U.S. cost-utility models published in the literature report incremental cost-effectiveness ratios of US$ 180,000-260,000 per quality-adjusted life-year, above conventional willingness-to-pay thresholds. Overall, semaglutide demonstrated marked cardiovascular risk reduction at all doses and across all populations, with low statistical heterogeneity. However, this benefit must be weighed against GI intolerance, limited racial and geographic representation and uncertain cost-effectiveness outside high-income regions. Future trials must oversample underrepresented minorities, extend to low- and middle-income regions, and include formal economic evaluations to further refine population-specific benefit-risk profiles and value estimates.

- PublicationType: Journal Article
- PubMed: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42347480/
- OA URL: https://www.mdpi.com/2075-4663/14/6/256/pdf?version=1782137626
- OpenAlex cited_by_count: 0

Abstract:
Data on menstrual health, energy availability, and injury risk in women undertaking extreme ultra-endurance expeditions remain limited. We conducted a prospective cohort study of the first all-female UK military team competing in a 3000-mile transatlantic rowing race, aiming to characterize menstrual function, low energy availability (LEA) risk, eating disorder (ED) risk, and injury profiles. Four female British Army personnel completed the 46-day race. Menstrual symptoms, injuries, and illnesses were recorded daily, while reproductive, inflammatory, biochemical, and hematological markers were assessed before and after the race. LEA and ED risk were evaluated using the Low Energy Availability in Females Questionnaire and Brief Eating Disorder in Athletes Questionnaire, respectively. Analyses were primarily descriptive. Three athletes experienced amenorrhea during the expedition, including one with previously regular cycles. The fourth reported intermittent abnormal bleeding associated with injury and illness and screened positive for LEA risk before and after the race. Another athlete screened positive for ED risk at both time points. Most biomarkers remained stable post-race, whereas reproductive hormones showed consistent reductions in follicle-stimulating hormone and luteinizing hormone in all four participants, alongside increased oestradiol. These findings, based on a sample of four athletes, suggest that menstrual function may be sensitive to sustained physiological stress in extreme ultra-endurance settings, and support prospective monitoring in female ultra-endurance, military, and expeditionary populations.

## ダイエット・筋トレ Reserve-20. Association Between Consumption of Energy and Sports Drinks with Oral Health: A Systematic Review.

- Candidate bucket: Reserve
- 事前スコア: 7
- PMID: 42345950
- DOI: 10.3390/dj14060359
- Journal: Dentistry journal
- PubDate: 2026-06-10
- PublicationType: Journal Article; Review
- PubMed: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42345950/
- OA URL: https://doi.org/10.3390/dj14060359
- OpenAlex cited_by_count: 0

Abstract:
: This study aimed to systematically review the association between the consumption of energy drinks and sports drinks with oral health. : A systematic search was conducted in three databases (PubMed, Web of Science and Embase) without any restrictions on publication year. Original studies (clinical trials, cohort, case-control studies and cross-sectional studies) reporting the association between energy drink or sports drink consumption and oral health or its impact on oral health were included. : The initial search found 1196 studies, and 10 studies with a total of 5805 participants (6-89 years old) met the inclusion criteria for analysis. Six studies investigated the association between energy drinks or sports drinks and dental erosion, whereas two studies reported dental caries outcomes and two studies reported saliva outcomes. Most (70%, 7/10) of the included studies were at high or serious risk of bias. Increased frequency or higher amounts of energy drink consumption were associated with a greater risk of dental erosion, whereas the relationship between sports drinks and dental erosion was inconsistent. Evidence regarding the association between dental caries experience and energy drink consumption was controversial, and no significant differences in caries experience were observed for sports drink consumption. : There was limited and low-quality evidence suggesting that consumption of energy drinks may be potentially associated with dental erosion experience, whereas findings related to dental caries were inconclusive. The association between sports drinks and dental erosion was inconsistent and supported by limited evidence. More well-designed studies on energy or sports drinks and oral health are needed to clarify these relationships.

- この枠は、筋トレ・ダイエット・抗老化領域のうち、一般読者にも話題化しやすい候補です。

- サプリ、動物実験、細胞実験、短期小規模研究は話題性があっても慎重に扱ってください。

### Interesting-1. Efficacy of Metformin in Prevention of Glucocorticoid-Induced Hyperglycemia in Patients Without Diabetes: A Meta-Analysis.
- Genre: 抗老化
- Interesting topic score: 15
- Quality score: 13
- PMID: 42332417
- DOI: 10.1002/edm2.70235
- Journal: Endocrinology, diabetes & metabolism
- Pub date: 2026-07-01
- Publication types: Journal Article; Meta-Analysis; Review
- PubMed URL: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42332417/
- Abstract: PURPOSE: The glucocorticoids are increasingly being used in the management of different autoimmune conditions and cancers. Our meta-analysis aims to leverage metformin's potential to reverse the metabolic complications of glucocorticoids by activating AMP-activated protein kinase (AMPK), while sparing their anti-inflammatory benefits.
METHODS: PubMed, Cochrane Library, trial registries and Google Scholar were searched from inception to June 2025 for Randomized Controlled Trials (RCTs) and observational studies comparing metformin and placebo to prevent metabolic side effects of glucocorticoid therapy in non-diabetic patients. After screening by two independent reviewers according to PRISMA guidelines, four studies involving 187 patients were analysed using the random-effects model in RevMan 5.4.1, and mean differences (MD) were calculated.
RESULTS: Preventive metformin administration during glucocorticoid treatment is superior to placebo with respect to glycaemic control as shown by statistically significant reduction in fasting blood glucose [MD = -0.60 (95% CI: -0.86 to -0.34)], HOMA index of insulin resistance [MD = -0.53 (95% CI: -0.97 to -0.08)], LDL levels [MD = -0.20 (95% CI: -0.40 to -0.00)] and total cholesterol [MD = -0.27 (95% CI: -0.54 to -0.01)]. However, our study failed to show significant improvement in area under the curve glucose (mmol/L × min) after challenge [MD = -176.66 (95% CI: -415.42, 62.11)], basal metabolic rate (BMR) [MD = 51.99 (95% CI: -53.08, 157.07)], HDL [MD = -0.04 (95% CI: -0.13, 0.05)], insulin levels [MD = -2.26 (95% CI: -5.90, 1.38)], triglycerides [MD = -0.15 (95% CI: -0.42, 0.13)] and body weight [MD = -0.93 (95% CI: -2.29 to 0.44)].
CONCLUSION: While glucocorticoids remain essential in various clinical contexts, their detrimental effects on glucose metabolism are well documented. This study supports metformin as a promising preventive treatment in non-diabetic patients receiving systemic glucocorticoid therapy. Improvement in insulin sensitivity and resulting fasting glucose levels may offset glucocorticoid-exacerbated inflammation. Further studies are needed to address long-term outcomes, including adiposity, bone metabolism, appetite, liver function and muscle wasting, as well as to identify possible predictors of therapeutic response.
TRIAL REGISTRATION: International Prospective Register of Systematic Reviews (PRO

### Interesting-2. Seaweed-Derived Extract Targets Porphyr'ageing to Modulate the Visible Signs of Aging in Human Skin.
- Genre: 抗老化
- Interesting topic score: 12
- Quality score: 10
- PMID: 42346805
- DOI: 10.3390/md24060220
- Journal: Marine drugs
- Pub date: 2026-06-18
- Publication types: Journal Article; Randomized Controlled Trial
- PubMed URL: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42346805/
- Abstract: Recent evidence suggests that microbiota-derived porphyrins contribute to skin aging, a phenomenon termed porphyr'aging. These pro-inflammatory molecules alter the expression of genes involved in senescence, trigger melanogenesis, and decrease collagen I synthesis in skin. The aim of this study was to evaluate the anti-aging properties of an upcycled extract (LHE) targeting bacterial porphyrins discovered after screening. The impact of LHE on porphyrin biosynthesis and on melanogenesis and wrinkles was evaluated using and tests and by conducting a double-blinded . placebo clinical trial. LHE significantly reduced coproporphyrin III production in Gram-positive skin bacteria and significantly decreased porphyrin levels at the skin surface. This activity was supported by a specific composition of LHE, comprising laminaran and mannitol. It also significantly decreased melanin content in skin explants and pigmentation in the clinical study (-5.9%). This effect was particularly pronounced in dark spots (ITA +39.9%), and the number of precursor spots also decreased (-6.9%). In addition, LHE significantly stimulated type I α-1 pro-collagen production in fibroblasts and increased collagen I and elastin expression in skin explants. These results were consistent with the clinical study, showing significant reductions in wrinkle number (-9.8%) and area (-5.8%). These findings suggest that targeting microbiota-derived porphyrins and their consequences may represent a promising approach to reduce the visible signs of aging.

### Interesting-3. Long-Term Safety and Renal Outcomes of Semaglutide in Non-Diabetic Obesity with Chronic Kidney Disease or Hypertension: A Systematic Review and Meta-Analysis.
- Genre: ダイエット・筋トレ
- Interesting topic score: 11
- Quality score: 13
- PMID: 42340790
- DOI: 10.7417/CT.2026.2083
- Journal: La Clinica terapeutica
- Pub date: 2026
- Publication types: Journal Article; Systematic Review
- PubMed URL: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42340790/
- Abstract: BACKGROUND: Semaglutide, a GLP-1 receptor agonist, has demonstrated metabolic and renal benefits in diabetic populations. However, its efficacy and safety in non-diabetic individuals with obesity and chronic kidney disease (CKD) remain largely unstudied. Given the high cardiometabolic risk in this group and limited therapeutic options, evaluating semaglutide's role is crucial.
OBJECTIVE: To assess the effects of semaglutide on body mass index (BMI), blood pressure, renal function (eGFR), and albuminuria in non-diabetic patients with obesity and CKD or hypertension.
METHODS: This systematic review and meta-analysis was conducted in accordance with PRISMA guidelines. A total of 580 studies were screened; 3 eligible studies (n=430 participants) were included. Data were extracted from a randomized controlled trial, a real-world observational dialysis study, and a large post hoc trial analysis. Fixed-effect meta-analysis models were applied to estimate pooled effects on BMI, systolic blood pressure (SBP), and renal outcomes.
RESULTS: Semaglutide treatment significantly reduced BMI (mean reduction: Tuttle 18.3%, Apperloo 11.8%, Vanek 1.5%; P = 0.001), and improved hypertension control (SBP <130 mmHg: Apperloo 20.6%, Vanek 12.5%, Tuttle 17.6%; P < 0.02). Renal function also improved, with eGFR >30 ml/min/1.73m² increasing from baseline in all studies (Apperloo 65.8%, Vanek 4.83%, Tuttle 36.4%; P < 0.001). No publication bias was detected.
CONCLUSIONS: Semaglutide is effective and well-tolerated in non-diabetic patients with obesity and CKD, resulting in significant weight loss, better blood pressure control, and improved renal parameters. These findings support its expanded use in non-diabetic CKD populations, including dialysis-dependent individuals.

## 1. Lifestyle interventions for dementia prevention in low- and middle-income countries: a systematic review.

- Date: 2026-06-24
- Genre: 抗老化
- Rank: 1
- Score: 78
- Importance level: high
- PMID: 42331514
- DOI: 10.1136/bmjgh-2024-017630
- Journal: BMJ Global Health
- Pub year: 2026
- Study design: システマティックレビュー・メタアナリシス
- Population: 低中所得国(LMIC)で認知症リスクを有する成人(対象研究数は要全文確認)
- Intervention: 多面的生活習慣介入(運動・食事・認知トレーニング・血管リスク管理等)
- Comparison: 通常ケアまたは非介入対照
- Main outcome: 認知機能・認知症発症リスク関連指標
- Key findings: LMICにおける多面的予防介入の効果と実装可能性を統合評価したSR/MA。具体的効果量とGRADE評価は要全文確認。
- Importance reason: 2050年までに認知症患者の約3分の2がLMICに集中する見込みで、予防介入の低資源環境への適用可能性を体系化した公衆衛生インパクトの大きいレビュー。
- Clinical relevance: 高所得国中心に開発された予防プログラムの移転可能性を検討する基礎資料。
- Novelty: 予防介入研究の地理的偏りに着目しLMIC適用を統合した点。
- Evidence strength: moderate
- Safety notes: 非侵襲的生活習慣介入が中心で重大な安全性懸念は小さい。
- Limitations: 対象研究の異質性・質のばらつき、LMIC内地域差。効果量・確実性は未確認。
- Practice change potential: moderate
- Next action: 全文で対象研究数・介入構成・効果量・確実性評価を確認する。
- Watch keywords: dementia prevention LMIC, multimodal lifestyle intervention, cognitive decline prevention, systematic review dementia

- Summary: LMICにおける認知症予防の多面的生活習慣介入を統合したSR/MA。実装可能性の検討に重点。
- Trend summary: 認知症予防研究の重心が高所得国から低中所得国の実装研究へ拡大している。
- Future outlook: LMIC現地で実施可能な低コスト多面的介入の大規模RCTと長期アウトカム検証が期待される。
- Deep dive: true

- Rank: 6

- Population: MASH（代謝機能関連脂肪肝炎）患者

- Evidence strength: moderate
- Safety notes: 各薬剤の安全性プロファイルをNMAで比較。消化器副作用・心血管リスクの差異を確認する必要がある。
- Limitations: 間接比較のため結果の不確実性あり。試験デザイン・アウトカム定義の異質性が影響する可能性。
- Practice change potential: MASH治療の処方最適化に直接影響する可能性が高い
- Next action: 全文でSGLT2阻害薬を含む組み合わせ療法の詳細ランキング・確実性評価・サブグループ別効果量を確認する

- OA URL: https://www.frontiersin.org/journals/endocrinology/articles/10.3389/fendo.2026.1829315/pdf
- Source URLs: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42325618/, https://doi.org/10.3389/fendo.2026.1829315
- Summary: MASH薬物療法のNMA。SGLT2阻害薬を含む最新治療薬をGLP-1RA・FGF21・THR-βと同一ネットワークで比較し、組み合わせ療法の有効性・安全性をランク付け。治療選択の実践的根拠を提供する包括的エビデンス統合研究。

- Evidence strength: moderate
- Safety notes: 単施設・短期フォローアップの限界あり。長期児の発達追跡データは未報告。

- Summary: 超高速卵子ガラス化保存（1分完了）と従来法の比較研究。臨床成績の同等性以上を示しつつscRNA-seqで分子レベルの品質を評価。Human Reproduction掲載でARTラボへの実装インパクトが高い。
- Trend summary: 卵子凍結技術の高速化・簡便化と分子レベルの品質担保を同時に検証するトレンドが加速している。

- Trend summary: 有酸素運動に加えレジスタンストレーニングの代謝疾患予防効果の証拠が蓄積されおり、ガイドライン改訂の動きが続いている。

- Date: 2026-06-23

- Rank: 7

- Study design: Systematic review / Meta-analysis
- Population: 妊婦（子癣妙症リスク集団）

- Safety notes: 脂質低下介入の妊娠中の安全性は別途評価が必要。スクリーニングとしての活用に留める。
- Limitations: 研究間の異質性（測定時期・脂質測定法の違い）。観察研究のみで因果関係は未確立。
- Practice change potential: 妊婦健诊での脂質スクリーニングの位置付け強化につながる可能性

- Summary: 血中脂質と子癣妙症リスクのメタ解析。高TG・高LDL・低HDLが子癣妙症リスクと有意に関連することを定量化。妊婦健诊での脂質スクリーニングを子癣妙症早期予測に統合する根拠となる。
- Trend summary: 妊娠初期の代謝マーカーによる子癣妙症予測研究が活発化。脂質・インスリン抗性・炎症マーカーの統合予測モデル構築へと進展している。

- Rank: 9
- Score: 54
- Importance level: moderate
- PMID: 42329333
- DOI: 10.1007/s40266-026-01310-z
- Journal: Drugs & Aging
- Pub year: 2026
- Study design: Systematic review / Meta-analysis（観察研究）
- Population: ガバペンチノイド（ガバペンチン・プレガバリン）使用成人
- Intervention: ガバペンチノイド長期使用
- Comparison: 非使用群
- Main outcome: アルツハイマー型認知症および関連認知症の発症リスク
- Key findings: ガバペンチノイド使用がアルツハイマー型認知症リスクと関連する可能性を示した。効果の方向性と大きさについてはスタディ間で一部差異あり。長期的認知機能への影響が活寻される。
- Importance reason: ガバペンチノイドは神経障害性疼痛・てんかん等で広く使用される薬剤で、認知症リスクとの関連は処方判断に直接影響する安全性シグナル。
- Clinical relevance: 高齢者への長期ガバペンチノイド処方の際に認知機能への影響を考慮するエビデンスとなる。

- Safety notes: 観察研究のみで交絡（適応症・他の薬剤）を完全に除去できない。因果関係は未確立。ただし高齢患者への長期処方では注意が必要。
- Limitations: 観察研究のみ。適応症による交絡が大きい。研究間の定義・フォローアップ期間の異質性。
- Practice change potential: 高齢者へのガバペンチノイド長期処方の慎重化を促す可能性
- Next action: 全文で効果量・信頼区間・交絡因子調整の詳細・薬剤別サブグループ（ガバペンチン vs プレガバリン）を確認する

- PubMed URL: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42329333/
- OA URL: 
- Source URLs: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42329333/
- Summary: ガバペンチノイドとアルツハイマー型認知症リスクのSR/MA（観察研究）。長期使用が認知症リスクと関連する可能性を示す安全性シグナル。高齢者への長期処方の注意嗚起として有用だが、因果関係は未確立。
- Trend summary: 高齢者への慢性疼痛治療薬の長期認知機能への影響研究が増加。ガバペンチノイドはその重点対象の一つとなっている。

## 22. Effects of Incretin-Based Therapies, Diet and Exercise Interventions, and Bariatric Surgery on Fat-Free Mass in Adults With Overweight or Obesity: A Systematic Review and Meta-Analysis

- Date: 2026-06-23
- Genre: ダイエット・筋トレ
- Rank: 10
- Score: 52
- Importance level: moderate
- PMID: 42324178
- DOI: 10.1111/dom.71006
- Journal: Diabetes, Obesity & Metabolism
- Pub year: 2026
- Study design: Systematic review / Meta-analysis
- Population: 過体重・肥満成人
- Intervention: インクレチン系薬物療法（GLP-1RA、GIP/GLP-1）、食事・運動介入、肥満外科手術
- Comparison: 介入法間の除脂肖体重（FFM）変化比較
- Main outcome: 除脂肖体重（FFM）変化
- Key findings: GLP-1RAは体重減少に伴い除脂肖体重も減少させる一方、運動介入の追加によりFFM損失が軽減される可能性を示した。肥満外科手術は最大のFFM損失と関連。食事＋運動の組み合わせが最もFFMを温存した。
- Importance reason: セマグルチド等の急速普及に伴い、体重減少の「質」（FFM保持）が臨床上重要な課題となっている。患者管理・運動処方への直接的示唆がある。
- Clinical relevance: GLP-1RA治療中の患者への運動処方追加の根拠となる。体組成管理の観点から診療計画に活用できる。
- Novelty: 最新のGIP/GLP-1二重作動薬を含むインクレチン系薬を包括FFMの観点でSR/MA評価した点。
- Evidence strength: moderate
- Safety notes: FFM損失は筋力低下・サルコペニアリスクと関連。長期的な機能的アウトカムへの影響は継続的な評価が必要。
- Limitations: 試験間のFFM測定法の異質性（DXA vs BIA等）。フォローアップ期間のばらつき。
- Practice change potential: GLP-1RA使用中の運動処方の標準化を促す可能性がある
- Next action: 全文でGLP-1RA vs GIP/GLP-1のFFM変化の差・運動追加による効果量・サルコペニア関連アウトカムを確認する
- Watch keywords: GLP-1RA lean mass, fat-free mass weight loss, incretin therapy body composition, bariatric surgery FFM, exercise GLP-1
- PubMed URL: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42324178/
- OA URL: 
- Source URLs: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42324178/
- Summary: GLP-1RA・食事運動・肥満外科手術の除脂肖体重（FFM）への影響 SR/MA。GLP-1RA使用時のFFM損失と運動追加による軽減効果を定量化。体組成管理の観点からGLP-1RA治療中の運動処方追加を支持するエビデンス。
- Trend summary: GLP-1RAの普及とともに体重減少の「質」（筋肉量保持）が重要テーマに浮上。運動との組み合わせ最適化研究が急増している。
- Future outlook: GIP/GLP-1二重作動薬（チルゼパチド等）のFFMへの影響と運動との最適組み合わせを検証した長期 RCTが期待される。

## 25. Mode of Anesthesia During Cesarean Section and Neonatal Morbidity and Mortality: A Cohort Study

- Date: 2026-06-22
- Genre: 周産期
- Rank: 1
- Score: 62
- Importance level: high
- PMID: 42305645
- DOI: 10.2147/LRA.S582928
- Journal: Local and regional anesthesia
- Pub year: 2026
- Study design: 後向きコホート研究
- Population: 2017-2021年に帝王切開を行った母体の新生児NICU入室例
- Intervention: 脊椎麻酔（SA）または全身麻酔（GA）での帝王切開
- Comparison: 全身麻酔 vs 脊椎麻酔
- Main outcome: 新生児罹患率・死亡率（NICU入室を含む）
- Key findings: 全身麻酔と脊椎麻酔の比較で新生児アウトカムの差を評価。緊急・待機例の両者を対象。SAが新生児アウトカムで有利な傾向を示す可能性。後向き単施設で交絡に限界あり。詳細は全文要確認。
- Importance reason: 帝王切開の麻酔選択は日常産科業務に直結。全身麻酔vs脊椎麻酔が新生児NICU入室・罹患に与える影響を実臨床データで検討しており、周産期管理プロトコル改善の参考になる。
- Clinical relevance: 産科麻酔選択の意思決定、特に緊急帝王切開での全身麻酔適応判断に関連。NICU管理方針の根拠となる可能性。
- Novelty: 2017-2021年の現代コホートで麻酔方法別の新生児アウトカムを包括評価した点。
- Evidence strength: low
- Safety notes: 後向きコホートで交絡制御に限界。単施設の可能性があり外的妥当性要確認。
- Limitations: 後向き観察研究、交絡因子の残存、緊急/待機の混在、単施設の可能性。因果関係は不明。
- Practice change potential: 中（プロトコル見直しのトリガーになりうる）
- Next action: 全文でサブグループ（緊急vs待機、母体合併症別）の効果推定値と交絡調整法を確認する。
- Watch keywords: cesarean anesthesia neonatal outcome, general anesthesia spinal anesthesia neonatal, NICU admission cesarean, obstetric anesthesia morbidity
- PubMed URL: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42305645/
- OA URL: https://doi.org/10.2147/lra.s582928
- Source URLs: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42305645/, https://doi.org/10.2147/lra.s582928
- Summary: 2017-2021年の後向きコホートで帝王切開時の麻酔方法（全身vs脊椎）が新生児NICU入室・罹患・死亡に与える影響を評価。日常産科麻酔選択に直結する臨床的関連性が高い。後向きで交絡に限界あり。
- Trend summary: 帝王切開の麻酔方法と新生児アウトカムの関連研究は継続的に報告されており、脊椎麻酔優位のエビデンス集積が続いている。
- Future outlook: 緊急帝王切開における全身麻酔適応の精緻化と、多施設前向き研究による因果推定が期待される。

- Date: 2026-06-22
- Genre: ダイエット・筋トレ
- Rank: 1
- Score: 82
- Importance level: high
- PMID: 42319968
- DOI: 10.1002/dmrr.70194
- Journal: Diabetes/Metabolism Research and Reviews
- Pub year: 2026
- Study design: Systematic Review and Meta-Analysis of RCTs
- Population: 肥満・2型糖尿病患者（RCT複数)
- Intervention: GLP-1RA（セマグルチド・リラグルチド等）またはSGLT2阻害薬
- Comparison: プラセボまたは対照群
- Main outcome: 除脂肪体重・脂肪量・体重変化
- Key findings: GLP-1RAは除脂肪体重を有意に減少させる一方、SGLT2阻害薬の影響は相対的に小さい。肥満・糖尿病患者での大規模減量薬使用に際し筋肉喪失リスクを定量化した初の包括的SR/MA。

- Evidence strength: moderate
- Safety notes: 除脂肪体重減少が筋機能低下・転倒リスクに繋がる可能性。長期的サルコペニアリスクへの影響は未確定。
- Limitations: RCT間の追跡期間・用量・測定法の異質性。DXA以外の体組成測定法を含む研究が混在。
- Practice change potential: GLP-1RA処方に筋肉喪失対策の運動指導を組み込む標準化を加速しうる。
- Next action: 全文でGLP-1RA種別・用量別の除脂肪体重変化量と異質性を確認。運動介入との比較サブグループがあれば抽出する。
- Watch keywords: GLP-1RA lean body mass, semaglutide muscle loss, SGLT2 inhibitor body composition, obesity pharmacotherapy sarcopenia
- PubMed URL: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42319968/
- OA URL: 
- Source URLs: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42319968/, https://doi.org/10.1002/dmrr.70194
- Summary: RCT SR/MAでGLP-1RAが除脂肪体重を有意に減少させることを示した。SGLT2阻害薬の影響は相対的に小さい。急拡大する減量薬処方において筋肉喪失リスクを定量化し、運動介入併用の必要性を支持する。PCOS・妊娠前肥満管理にも直接波及する重要エビデンス。
- Trend summary: GLP-1RA使用拡大に伴い筋肉喪失・骨密度低下への懸念が高まっており、体組成への影響を定量化するSR/MAが相次いでいる。
- Future outlook: GLP-1RA＋抵抗性運動の最適併用プロトコルを検討する大規模RCTが必要。産婦人科集団での特化した検討も期待される。
- Deep dive: true
- Deep dive reason: GLP-1RA処方が急拡大する中、筋肉喪失リスク定量化は産婦人科・肥満外来を含む多科横断的な実装判断に直結するため。

- Novelty: 自然周期vs人工周期のRCTとしてHuman Reproduction掲載の最新エビデンス。
- Evidence strength: high
- Safety notes: 自然周期ではLHサージのタイミング管理が必要で、排卵検出の見落としリスクに注意。人工周期には血栓リスクのエストロゲン投与が含まれる。
- Limitations: 単施設または限定施設；排卵女性のみへの適用で無排卵・PCOS患者への外挿は不可。
- Practice change potential: 排卵女性のFETでは自然周期を第一選択として標準化するプロトコル変更の根拠となりうる。
- Next action: 全文でLHサージ検出プロトコル・補足的黄体サポート有無・OHSS既往例への対応を確認。施設プロトコルとの比較検討。
- Watch keywords: FET natural cycle RCT, frozen embryo transfer protocol, endometrial preparation ovulatory, artificial cycle HRT
- PubMed URL: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42315758/
- OA URL: 
- Source URLs: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42315758/, https://doi.org/10.1093/humrep/deag095
- Summary: 排卵女性のFETで自然周期と人工周期の臨床妊娠率が同等であることを示したRCT。自然周期は薬剤負担軽減と生理的内膜環境の観点から支持される。排卵機能のある患者への不要なホルモン投与を回避できるプロトコル転換の根拠。
- Trend summary: FETの内膜準備法については自然周期を支持するエビデンスが蓄積しており、特に排卵女性での自然周期優先の流れが加速している。
- Future outlook: PCOS・無排卵患者を含む幅広い集団への適用可能性と、妊娠・周産期アウトカムの長期比較研究が必要。
- Deep dive: true
- Deep dive reason: 生殖医療の日常プロトコルを直接変えうるRCTで、Human Reproductionのエビデンスとして実装判断に最直結するため。

## 29. Rethinking parenteral nutrition as supportive therapy for neonatal sepsis

- Date: 2026-06-22
- Genre: 周産期
- Rank: 3
- Score: 48
- Importance level: moderate
- PMID: 42302786
- DOI: 10.1016/j.medj.2026.101182
- Journal: Med (New York, N.Y.)
- Pub year: 2026
- Study design: Perspective・レビュー
- Population: 新生児（特に早産児）の敗血症患者
- Intervention: 非経口栄養（PN）の組成・タイミング最適化（免疫代謝的視点）
- Comparison: 従来のグルコース高含有PNと免疫調整型PNの概念比較
- Main outcome: 炎症制御・臓器傷害・臨床アウトカム（概念的）
- Key findings: 新生児敗血症に対するPNのガイドラインが不在。高グルコースPNは過剰な解糖系依存免疫応答を誘導しうる。免疫代謝学的観点からPNが炎症・臓器傷害を修飾しうるという概念的転換を提唱。
- Importance reason: NICU管理でガイドラインが存在しない空白領域に問題提起。免疫代謝学的視点からの栄養戦略は今後の研究方向性を示す。
- Clinical relevance: 新生児敗血症のNICU管理、特に非経口栄養処方の見直し議論に関連。
- Novelty: 免疫代謝学的メカニズムを用いてPNの組成が新生児免疫応答を能動的に制御できると主張した点。
- Evidence strength: low
- Safety notes: Perspectiveであり一次臨床データなし。前臨床モデルへの依存が大きい。
- Limitations: 一次データなし、前臨床モデル依存、ヒト新生児への外挿は要注意、無作為化試験なし。
- Practice change potential: 低（概念提唱段階、今後の研究待ち）
- Next action: 引用されている前臨床モデルのデータとヒト観察研究の質を確認する。
- Watch keywords: neonatal sepsis parenteral nutrition, immunometabolism neonatal nutrition, glucose parenteral nutrition inflammation, preterm sepsis nutritional support
- PubMed URL: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42302786/
- OA URL: 
- Source URLs: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42302786/
- Summary: 新生児敗血症（特に早産児）における非経口栄養のガイドライン不在を問題提起するPerspective。高グルコースPNが免疫応答を過剰刺激しうるという免疫代謝学的概念転換を提唱。ヒト一次データはなく前臨床モデル依存。
- Trend summary: 新生児集中治療における栄養の免疫調節作用への関心が高まっている。
- Future outlook: 新生児敗血症に対する免疫代謝最適化PNの臨床試験設計が期待される。
- Deep dive: 
- Deep dive reason: Perspectiveであり一次データなし。概念的な問題提起にとどまる。

## 30. Plasma proteomic signatures of cellular aging predict human disease

- Date: 2026-06-22
- Genre: 抗老化
- Rank: 3
- Score: 78
- Importance level: high
- PMID: 42297981
- DOI: 10.1038/s41591-026-04446-y
- Journal: Nature Medicine
- Pub year: 2026
- Study design: 大規模コホート研究（機械学習・プロテオミクス）
- Population: 60,542例（血漿プロテオーム測定）
- Intervention: 細胞型特異的老化シグネチャーの血漿プロテオーム推定
- Comparison: 暦年齢・従来の老化バイオマーカー
- Main outcome: 細胞型別老化スコアによる疾患予測精度
- Key findings: 7,000超の血漿タンパク質から機械学習モデルで細胞型別老化スコアを構築。スコアは将来の疾患発症を予測し、老化が臓器・細胞種によって非同期であることを大規模に実証。
- Importance reason: 60,542例という超大規模サンプルでの血液ベース老化バイオマーカー確立はNature Medicine水準の突破口。非侵襲的な老化評価と疾患予測の新規アプローチを提示。
- Clinical relevance: 血液検査のみで個人の細胞型別老化プロファイルを評価し、疾患リスク層別化や抗老化介入の効果モニタリングへの応用が期待される。
- Novelty: 細胞型特異的老化を血漿プロテオームで推定した点。7,000超タンパク質・60,542例は前例のない規模。
- Evidence strength: moderate
- Safety notes: 観察研究のため因果推論不可。臨床実装前にvalidation・コスト評価が必要。
- Limitations: 観察研究；コホートの人種・社会経済的多様性；7,000タンパク測定の実臨床コスト；臨床実装への距離がある。
- Practice change potential: 将来的に血液1本で老化プロファイルを評価する標準検査への道を開く可能性。
- Next action: 全文でvalidation cohortの詳細・細胞型別スコアの構成タンパク質・疾患予測のAUCを確認。
- Watch keywords: plasma proteomics aging, cellular aging biomarker, Nature Medicine aging, biological age prediction
- PubMed URL: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42297981/
- OA URL: https://doi.org/10.1038/s41591-026-04446-y
- Source URLs: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42297981/, https://doi.org/10.1038/s41591-026-04446-y
- Summary: 60,542例の血漿プロテオームから細胞型別老化スコアを機械学習で構築し、疾患予測に有用であることを示したNature Medicine掲載の大規模研究。老化の非同期性を臓器・細胞レベルで実証。血液ベースの老化評価と疾患リスク層別化への新しいアプローチ。
- Trend summary: 血液ベースの老化バイオマーカー研究が急速に進展しており、プロテオミクスによる生物学的年齢推定が疾患予測に応用される流れが加速。
- Future outlook: マルチオミクス統合や介入試験への応用、および測定コスト低下による実臨床導入が期待される。

- Deep dive reason:

- Date: 2026-06-22
- Genre: ダイエット・筋トレ
- Rank: 4
- Score: 45
- Importance level: moderate
- PMID: 42302891
- DOI: 10.1016/j.joca.2026.06.004
- Journal: Osteoarthritis and cartilage
- Pub year: 2026
- Study design: RCT基盤の横断解析（FEAST trial、n=144）
- Population: 膝OA患者144例（平均年齢65歳、BMI30.3、64%女性）
- Intervention: DXAによる総体脂肪・内臓脂肪の定量評価

- Novelty: 膝OAでDXAによる内臓脂肪を性差別に評価した点。BMI超えた指標の重要性を示す。
- Evidence strength: moderate
- Safety notes: 横断解析で因果不明。n=144で検出力に限界。
- Limitations: 横断解析（ベースラインデータのみ）、n=144と小規模、単施設の可能性。
- Practice change potential: 低〜中（体組成評価の重要性を支持するが、実装には追加エビデンスが必要）
- Next action: FEASTトライアルの縦断アウトカムデータで介入による内臓脂肪減少と膝OA改善の関連を確認する。
- Watch keywords: visceral adiposity knee osteoarthritis sex-specific, body composition OA outcomes DXA, FEAST trial osteoarthritis adiposity, fat mass knee pain sex difference
- PubMed URL: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42302891/
- OA URL: https://doi.org/10.1016/j.joca.2026.06.004
- Source URLs: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42302891/, https://doi.org/10.1016/j.joca.2026.06.004
- Summary: 膝OA患者144例のRCT基盤横断解析。DXAで内臓脂肪を定量し臨床アウトカムとの関連を性差別評価。男性で内臓脂肪の影響が強く、BMI超えた体組成評価の有用性を示唆。n小規模で限界あり。
- Trend summary: 肥満関連疾患でBMIを超えた体脂肪組成評価（特に内臓脂肪）と性差の重要性が注目されている。
- Future outlook: 内臓脂肪減少介入（食事・運動）が膝OA臨床アウトカムを改善するかの大規模RCTが期待される。
- Deep dive: 
- Deep dive reason: 横断解析で小規模（n=144）。概念的に興味深いが因果関係不明。

- Trend summary: 血液バイオマーカーによるAD早期診断の精度向上が急速に進んでおり、p-Tau217が国際的スタンダードとして台頭しつつある。

- Comparison: 正常体重 vs 過体重 vs 肥満（乱視発症リスク）
- Main outcome: 乱視の新規発症（縦断）
- Key findings: 小児肥満・過体重が乱視リスクと有意に関連。大規模コホートで縦断的に初めて評価。BMI増加に伴う乱視リスクの上昇を確認。
- Importance reason: 小児肥満の端科的合併症という新規アウトカムを大規模縦断コホートで評価。学校健診・小児科での体重管理の意義を支持する可能性。
- Clinical relevance: 小児肥満管理の議論に端科的合併症という新たな観点を追加。
- Novelty: 小児肥満と乱視の縦断的関連を大規模コホートで初評価した点（ネタ枚）。
- Evidence strength: moderate
- Safety notes: 後向きコホートで因果不明。乱視判定基準の統一性を確認要。
- Limitations: 後向き、因果不明、交絡（遙伝・環境）、単一保険データで一般化に限界。
- Practice change potential: 低（仮説生成的、追加検証が必要）
- Next action: 乱視のメカニズム仮説（眼窝脂肪・眼圧）と交絡調整の詳細を全文で確認する。
- Watch keywords: childhood obesity astigmatism longitudinal, BMI refractive error children, pediatric overweight eye astigmatism, body mass index vision children
- PubMed URL: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42302853/
- OA URL: 
- Source URLs: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42302853/
- Summary: イスラエル6-10歳兩22,130人の後向きコホートで小児肥満・過体重と乱視発症リスクを縦断評価。BMI増加に伴う乱視リスク上昇を初めて大規模に確認。後向きで因果不明。ネタ枚候補。
- Trend summary: 小児肥満の全身合併症研究が端科・整形外科など多領域に拡大している。
- Future outlook: 小児肥満介入が乱視発症を予防するかの前向き研究が期待される。

- Deep dive reason: ネタ枚。大規模コホートだが後向きで因果不明、直接的臨床変更には至らない。

- Date: 2026-06-22

- Rank: 7
- Score: 70

- PMID: 42311541

- Trend summary: GDM早期予測バイオマーカーの探索が活発化しており、既存検査の再利用が注目されている。

- Date: 2026-06-22
- Genre: ダイエット・筋トレ
- Rank: 8
- Score: 68
- Importance level: moderate
- PMID: 42309659
- DOI: 10.1136/bmjopen-2025-098765
- Journal: BMJ Open
- Pub year: 2026
- Study design: Network Meta-Analysis
- Population: 過体重・肥満女性
- Intervention: 各種運動介入（有酸素・筋トレ・HIIT・複合）
- Comparison: 運動なし対照群・介入間比較
- Main outcome: 体脂肪率・除脂肪体重・BMI・腹囲
- Key findings: 複合運動（有酸素＋筋トレ）が体脂肪減少と除脂肪体重維持に最も効果的。HIITは時間効率が高い。いずれも有酸素単独より体組成改善に優れる。

- Evidence strength: moderate
- Safety notes: 強度の高いHIITは初心者・高齢者への適応に注意。
- Limitations: 研究間の介入プロトコル・測定法・追跡期間の異質性；ネットワークの一貫性評価が限定的。
- Practice change potential: 複合運動を女性肥満管理の第一推奨として標準化する根拠となりうる。
- Next action: 全文で運動種別ごとのSMD・介入期間・コンプライアンス率を確認。GLP-1RA群との比較があれば抽出。

- PubMed URL: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42309659/
- OA URL: https://doi.org/10.1136/bmjopen-2025-098765
- Source URLs: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42309659/, https://doi.org/10.1136/bmjopen-2025-098765
- Summary: 過体重・肥満女性への運動介入のNMAで複合運動（有酸素＋筋トレ）が体脂肪減少と除脂肪体重維持に最も効果的であることを示した。GLP-1RA処方時の運動併用戦略策定に直結するエビデンス。
- Trend summary: 女性の体組成改善に向けた最適運動様式の特定が進んでおり、個別化運動処方の普及が加速している。

- Genre: 周産期
- Rank: 11
- Score: 63
- Importance level: moderate
- PMID: 42314205
- DOI: 10.1097/AOG.0000000000005801
- Journal: Obstetrics & Gynecology
- Pub year: 2026
- Study design: Narrative Review
- Population: 妊婦・女性一般（レビュー）
- Intervention: 気候変動関連暴露（熱波・大気汚染・山火事の煙）
- Comparison: なし（レビュー）
- Main outcome: 流産・早産・子焃前症・児発育への影響
- Key findings: 熱波・大気汚染・山火事の煙と流産・早産・子焃前症・SGAのリスク上昇を総合的に整理。OBGYN視点から気候変動の健康影響をまとめた初の包括的レビューの一つ。
- Importance reason: Obstetrics & Gynecology掲載で実証性の高い政策的テーマ。許容地域での山火事暴露・熱波への対応指针として現場医師にも実用的。
- Clinical relevance: 山火事・熱波リスクの高い地域での妊婦管理における暗默のリスク認識と患者指導の根拠となる。
- Novelty: 産婦人科視点から複数の気候変動要因を統合したレビュー。
- Evidence strength: low
- Safety notes: 気候変動暴露と周産期アウトカムの因果推論は限定的。観察的・生態学的エビデンスに基づく。
- Limitations: ナラティブレビューで因果推論不可；地域・コホート間の気候暴露の定義標準の遠い。
- Practice change potential: 気候変動リスクを妊婦健診の問診項目に追加することを促す可能性。
- Next action: 全文で地域別・暑炒別のリスク比と予防から丫介策を確認。
- Watch keywords: climate change pregnancy outcomes, wildfire smoke preterm birth, heat wave obstetric, air pollution preeclampsia
- PubMed URL: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42314205/
- OA URL: 
- Source URLs: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42314205/
- Summary: 気候変動関連暴露（熱波・大気汚染・山火事の煙）と流産・早産・子焃前症のリスク上昇を総合したObstetrics & Gynecologyのレビュー。ネイティブレビューで因果推論は限定的だが政策的インパクトは高い。
- Trend summary: 気候変動と母児保健の関連性に関する論文が急増しており、OBGYN分野での検討が本格化している。
- Future outlook: 地域別・季節別の気候変動暴露と周産期アウトカムの定量的解析と介入試験設計が期待される。

## 44. Weight-loss drugs for adults with hypertension: a Cochrane systematic review

- Date: 2026-06-22
- Genre: ダイエット・筋トレ
- Rank: 12
- Score: 61
- Importance level: moderate
- PMID: 42316203
- DOI: 10.1002/14651858.CD015234.pub2
- Journal: Cochrane Database of Systematic Reviews
- Pub year: 2026
- Study design: Cochrane Systematic Review
- Population: 高血圧を有する肉満・肥満成人
- Intervention: 減量薬（オルリスタット・GLP-1RA・ナルトレキソン・ブプロピオン等）
- Comparison: プラセボまたは生活習慣改善のみ
- Main outcome: 血圧・体重・心血管イベント・副作用
- Key findings: 複数の減量薬が血圧を有意に低下させるが副作用プロファイルは薬剤間で異なる。GLP-1RAは心血管イベント低減に有意なデータ。Cochrane水準の証拠として補完する重要文献。
- Importance reason: CochraneレベルのSRとして最高エビデンスグレードかつ高血圧合併の肉満・肥満患者によく遇う産婦人科外来にも実用的。
- Clinical relevance: 高血圧合併肥満患者への減量薬選択と副作用カウンセリングの根拠となる。PCOS・代謝症候群を持つ女性の長期管理にも波及。
- Novelty: GLP-1RAを含む最新減量薬群を網羅したCochrane SR。
- Evidence strength: high
- Safety notes: 減量薬の血圧低下効果の一方で、達成遠慄・インスリン頭痛・消化器副作用に注意。妊娠中使用は原則禁忌。
- Limitations: RCT間の投与期間・追跡期間・イベント定義の差異；女性・少数民族のサブグループ解析は限定的。
- Practice change potential: 高血圧合併肥満へのGLP-1RA適応を支持する最高水準エビデンス。
- Next action: 全文でGLP-1RA別の血圧低下効果量・心血管イベントサブグループ・副作用比較を確認。
- Watch keywords: weight loss drug hypertension, GLP-1RA blood pressure, obesity antihypertensive, Cochrane weight management
- PubMed URL: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42316203/
- OA URL: https://doi.org/10.1002/14651858.CD015234.pub2
- Source URLs: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42316203/, https://doi.org/10.1002/14651858.CD015234.pub2
- Summary: Cochrane SRで高血圧合併肉満・肥満成人への減量薬が血圧を有意に低下させ、GLP-1RAは心血管イベント低減にも有意なデータを示すことを示した。高血圧合併肥満へのGLP-1RA適応を支持する最高水準エビデンス。
- Trend summary: GLP-1RAの高血圧改善効果は登録若枕の考慮事項に加わりつつあり、減量・心血管両方を考慮した蓄積的エビデンスが引き続き重要。
- Future outlook: 高血圧合併肥満への専用設計RCTと、血圧降下薬とGLP-1RAの併用対分析が期待される。
- Deep dive: 
- Deep dive reason: 

## 45. Postpartum haemorrhage: epidemiology, consequences, and missed opportunities

- Date: 2026-06-21
- Genre: 周産期
- Rank: 1
- Score: 88
- Importance level: 高
- PMID: 42285119
- DOI: 10.1016/S0140-6736(26)00902-5
- Journal: Lancet
- Pub year: 2026
- Study design: レビュー（Lancet PPHシリーズ）
- Population: 産後出血を生じうる全分娩女性
- Intervention: PPHの疫学・予防・診断・治療の包括的整理とWHO新定義の提示
- Comparison: 従来定義・従来管理
- Main outcome: PPH発生・死亡・経済負担とWHO新定義
- Key findings: 年間約2700万人にPPH、約4万3000人が死亡；膣分娩有病率12.6%、帝切30.9%；WHOが客観測定出血300mL＋血行動態異常または500mLへ再定義
- Importance reason: PPHの定義・予防・診断を診療レベルで更新しうる主要Lancetレビュー。WHO新定義と見逃しの体系的整理
- Clinical relevance: 周産期出血管理プロトコルとリスク評価の見直しに直結
- Novelty: WHO新定義と見逃し体系整理
- Evidence strength: moderate
- Safety notes: レビューであり各推奨は一次データ遡及確認が必要
- Limitations: 一次研究ではなく統合レビュー；推奨根拠強度は項目差
- Practice change potential: 高
- Next action: WHO新定義の国内実装状況とcalibrated drape導入効果を追跡する
- Watch keywords: postpartum haemorrhage WHO definition, PPH prevention uterotonic, calibrated drape, maternal mortality PPH
- PubMed URL: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42285119/
- OA URL: 
- Source URLs: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42285119/, https://doi.org/10.1016/S0140-6736(26)00902-5
- Summary: Lancetの産後出血レビュー。年間2700万人に発生し4万3000人が死亡。WHOが出血量＋血行動態に基づく新定義を提示し早期診断治療を重視。
- Trend summary: PPHは客観的血液量測定と新定義による早期診断へと管理潮流が移行している。
- Future outlook: WHO新定義の世界的実装とバンドル治療の標準化が進むと見込まれる。
- Deep dive: true
- Deep dive reason: WHOのPPH新定義と予防戦略は実臨床の出血管理を変えうるため深掘りが必要

- Trend summary: 予防はリスク層別化と単剤標準化、供給確保へと向かっている。
- Future outlook: 低資源環境での予防実装と熱安定カルベトシン普及が焦点。

- Key findings: PGT-Aは初回（OR0.86）および累積（OR0.74）生児獲得率の低下と関連、流産は減少（累積OR0.64）、48%で初回移植に至らず

- Clinical relevance: PGT-Aの適応とカウンセリングに直接影響

- Evidence strength: moderate
- Safety notes: 胚生検の侵襲・移植機会損失の論点
- Limitations: 観察研究；2014〜2018年で技術が現行と異なる可能性；交絡残存
- Practice change potential: 中〜高
- Next action: 現行NGS・モザイク胚を含む前向きRCTと併せて解釈する
- Watch keywords: PGT-A live birth rate, HFEA register, aneuploidy testing IVF, embryo biopsy outcome
- PubMed URL: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42275751/
- OA URL: 
- Source URLs: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42275751/, https://doi.org/10.1016/j.rbmo.2026.105747
- Summary: 英国HFEAレジストリ解析でPGT-Aはルーチン診療下で累積生児獲得率を下げ流産を減らすと示した。全例適用の有用性に疑問。
- Trend summary: PGT-Aは全例適用から特定層への限定運用へ議論が移行している。
- Future outlook: 現行技術での前向きRCTとサブグループ別適応の精緻化が進む。
- Deep dive: true
- Deep dive reason: PGT-Aの全例適用に不利な大規模証拠で適応判断を変えうるため深掘りが必要

- Summary: 27研究のメタアナリシス。妊娠前後の肝酵素上昇がGDMリスクと関連し、GGT(OR2.57)とHSI(OR2.19)が強い。異質性高・証拠確実性 very low で臨床応用は限定的。

## 58. The Texas Abortion Ban and Maternal Mental Health

- Date: 2026-06-20
- Genre: 周産期
- Rank: 2
- Score: 80
- Importance level: high
- PMID: 42313383
- DOI: 10.1001/jamanetworkopen.2026.19396
- Journal: JAMA Network Open
- Pub year: 2026
- Study design: Repeated cross-sectional study, difference-in-differences (DiD)
- Population: US mothers aged 18-49 (Texas n=4,323; non-ban states n=152,573)
- Intervention: Implementation of Texas SB8 (abortion ban, September 2021)
- Comparison: Mothers in states without abortion bans
- Main outcome: Self-reported fair or poor mental/emotional health
- Key findings: +2.52 pp increase in poor mental health post-SB8 (95%CI 0.02-5.01); largest in mothers with publicly insured children (+7.06 pp)
- Importance reason: 大規模DiD設計でAbortion政策が母体メンタルヘルスを悪化させることを示した。政策議論と周産期精神医学両面で引用される重要研究
- Clinical relevance: 政策環境が母体精神健康に与える影響を示す。日本の生殖医療・中絶政策議論の参照点
- Novelty: 国家規模サーベイを用いたDiD設計でAbortion政策の母体メンタルヘルス影響を定量化
- Evidence strength: moderate
- Safety notes: 横断反復デザインで個人追跡なし；テキサス特有の残存交絡あり
- Limitations: 横断反復デザインで因果確定は困難；テキサス固有の交絡；父親メンタルへの感度分析で有意差なく母体特異性を示唆
- Practice change potential: 中（政策・カウンセリング実践への影響大）
- Next action: 他州・他政策での類似研究と中長期追跡による因果関係確認
- Watch keywords: abortion ban maternal mental health, Texas SB8, reproductive policy mental health, Dobbs decision outcomes
- PubMed URL: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42313383/
- OA URL: 
- Source URLs: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42313383/
- Summary: JAMA Network OpenのDiD研究。SB8後テキサス州母親の精神的不健康が+2.52 pp増加。公的保険加入児の母親で最大+7.06 pp。政策影響の重要な定量的証拠。
- Trend summary: 生殖政策と母体健康アウトカムを疫学的に評価する研究が急増。
- Future outlook: 他の禁止政策・州への一般化と長期精神健康・母子アウトカムの追跡が必要。
- Deep dive: 
- Deep dive reason: 政策研究で直接診療を変えるわけではないが重要

- Rank: 4

- Importance level: high
- PMID: 42312200
- DOI: 10.3389/fendo.2026.1850346
- Journal: Frontiers in Endocrinology

- Study design: Prospective cohort
- Population: 680 infertile patients undergoing IVF cycles
- Intervention: Serum and follicular fluid oxytocin measurement
- Comparison: Levels across quartiles
- Main outcome: Live birth rate (LBR) following fresh embryo transfer
- Key findings: Each 100 pg/mL increase in serum oxytocin decreased LBR by 37% (95%CI 25-47%); follicular fluid oxytocin increase of 100 pg/mL improved LBR by 18% (95%CI 2-37%)
- Importance reason: IVF前の血清オキシトシンが生児獲得率の独立した負の予測因子であることを680例前向きコホートで示した。新規バイオマーカー候補として価値大
- Clinical relevance: IVF患者のカウンセリングやプロトコル選択における新しい予後評価指標の候補
- Novelty: 血清と卵胞液オキシトシンの方向が逆の関連を示した点は新知見
- Evidence strength: moderate
- Safety notes: 観察研究で介入なし
- Limitations: 前向きコホートだが単施設；因果関係は未確立；測定タイミングの標準化が課題
- Practice change potential: 中（バイオマーカーとしての前向き多施設検証が必要）
- Next action: 多施設前向き研究でのバイオマーカー再現性確認と閾値最適化
- Watch keywords: serum oxytocin IVF, follicular fluid oxytocin, live birth predictor ART, oxytocin metabolic syndrome IVF
- PubMed URL: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42312200/
- OA URL: https://www.frontiersin.org/journals/endocrinology/articles/10.3389/fendo.2026.1850346/pdf
- Source URLs: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42312200/
- Summary: 680例前向きコホート。血清オキシトシン100 pg/mL増でLBR 37%低下、卵胞液オキシトシンは18%改善。血清オキシトシンはTG・LDL・インスリンと正相関しメタボリック因子との関連が示唆。
- Trend summary: IVFの予後バイオマーカー研究が血清内分泌指標の方向に拡大している。
- Future outlook: 多施設でのバイオマーカー検証と介入による転帰改善の探索が期待される。
- Deep dive: true
- Deep dive reason: 680例の前向きコホートで生児獲得率と強く関連し、IVF予後評価の新指標として実装可能性があるため

## 63. Efficacy of Less Invasive Surfactant Administration (LISA) in Preterm Neonates With Respiratory Distress Syndrome: A Systematic Review and Meta-Analysis

- Date: 2026-06-20
- Genre: 周産期
- Rank: 7
- Score: 66
- Importance level: high
- PMID: 42311598
- DOI: 10.1177/30502225261453435
- Journal: Sage Open Pediatrics
- Pub year: 2026
- Study design: Systematic review and meta-analysis (21 RCTs, 2,656 infants)
- Population: Preterm infants with RDS
- Intervention: LISA (less invasive surfactant administration)
- Comparison: INSURE (intubation-surfactant-extubation)
- Main outcome: BPD, death, BPD or death, intubation/MV, severe IVH
- Key findings: LISA associated with lower odds of BPD, death, BPD-or-death, intubation/MV, and severe IVH; greater benefit in <=34 weeks and high antenatal steroid exposure
- Importance reason: 21RCT・2656例のメタアナリシスでLISAのINSURE比優位性を確認。サブグループ別の適応最適化に寄与
- Clinical relevance: NICUでのサーファクタン投与法選択の標準化根拠
- Novelty: サブグループ別（在胎週数・ステロイド曝露）の効果修飾を定量化
- Evidence strength: high
- Safety notes: LISA手技の習熟度依存；施設間で成績差あり
- Limitations: 試験間異質性；長期神経発達アウトカムは限定的
- Practice change potential: 中（NICUプロトコルへの統合）
- Next action: <=34週・高ステロイド曝露例でのLISAプロトコル標準化と長期アウトカム追跡
- Watch keywords: LISA INSURE preterm surfactant, BPD surfactant administration, less invasive surfactant, neonatal respiratory distress
- PubMed URL: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42311598/
- OA URL: https://doi.org/10.1177/30502225261453435
- Source URLs: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42311598/
- Summary: 21RCT・2656例のメタアナリシス。LISAはINSURE比でBPD・死亡・重症IVHを低減。在胎34週以下と高ステロイド曝露例でより大きな効果を確認。
- Trend summary: LISAの有効性証拠が積み上がり低侵襲サーファクタン投与の標準化が進む。
- Future outlook: 長期神経発達と施設間普及のギャップを埋める実装研究が期待される。
- Deep dive: 
- Deep dive reason: Reserve候補だが高質エビデンスで選定

## 64. Opposing effects of PM2.5 on TSH levels: effect modification by thyroid peroxidase antibody status in a preconception cohort

- Date: 2026-06-20
- Genre: 周産期
- Rank: 8
- Score: 62
- Importance level: moderate
- PMID: 42312203
- DOI: 10.3389/fendo.2026.1818739
- Journal: Frontiers in Endocrinology
- Pub year: 2026
- Study design: Prospective cohort (China Medical University Birth Cohort)
- Population: 1,357 women planning pregnancy (Liaoning, China, 2019-2023)
- Intervention: PM2.5 exposure (1-12 month windows)
- Comparison: TPOAb-positive vs TPOAb-negative subgroups
- Main outcome: TSH levels
- Key findings: 10 ug/m3 PM2.5 increase decreased TSH in TPOAb-negative (beta -0.074) but increased TSH in TPOAb-positive women (beta +0.156); interaction p=0.003; effect most pronounced at 6-month window
- Importance reason: PM2.5の甲状腺影響がTPOAb状態で方向が逆転するという新知見は環境内分泌研究の方法論に影響する
- Clinical relevance: 妊活中のTPOAb陽性女性を環境感受性サブグループとして識別する根拠の可能性
- Novelty: PM2.5×TPOAb交互作用でTSH変化の方向が逆転する現象を示した点
- Evidence strength: moderate
- Safety notes: 単一中国コホートで一般化に限界
- Limitations: 中国単一コホート；PM2.5は推定値；TSH変化の臨床的意義は未確立
- Practice change potential: 低〜中（環境内分泌研究の方法論への影響は大）
- Next action: 他コホートでのTPOAb別PM2.5影響の再現性確認
- Watch keywords: PM2.5 thyroid TSH, TPOAb PM2.5 interaction, air pollution thyroid autoimmunity, preconception thyroid environment
- PubMed URL: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42312203/
- OA URL: https://www.frontiersin.org/journals/endocrinology/articles/10.3389/fendo.2026.1818739/pdf
- Source URLs: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42312203/
- Summary: 1357例の妊活前コホート。PM2.5増加でTPOAb陰性はTSH低下、陽性はTSH上昇と方向が逆転（交互作用p=0.003）。TPOAb陽性女性が環境感受性サブグループである可能性を示す。
- Trend summary: PM2.5の内分泌撹乱影響が個人の自己免疫㋌武用で修飾されるという研究視点が注目されている。
- Future outlook: 他コホートでの再現検証と妊娠転帰への影響評価が期待される。
- Deep dive: 
- Deep dive reason: 新規性高いが即時臨床応用には限定的

## 69. A comparison of the safety of oral labetalol versus nifedipine to manage hypertension in pregnancy in Australia: a target trial emulation

- Date: 2026-06-18
- Genre: 周産期
- Rank: 1
- Score: 88
- Importance level: critical
- PMID: 42306491
- DOI: 10.1016/j.eclinm.2026.104002
- Journal: EClinicalMedicine
- Pub year: 2026
- Study design: Target trial emulation (retrospective cohort, doubly-robust IPWRA)
- Population: 7,416妊娠例（妊娠高血圧・子癇前症・慢性高血圧）、オーストラリア・ビクトリア州2009-2020
- Intervention: ラベタロール経口（n=6,745）
- Comparison: ニフェジピン経口（n=671）
- Main outcome: 母体複合アウトカム（死亡・重篤罹患）、新生児複合アウトカム
- Key findings: ニフェジピン群で母体複合アウトカムリスク33%増加（aRR 1.33, 95%CI 1.07-1.64）。子癇・HELLP症候群・腎不全増加が主因。新生児アウトカムに有意差なし。

- Novelty: ターゲットトライアルエミュレーションによる7,416例規模の比較。交絡調整後もニフェジピン不良アウトカム残存が新知見。
- Evidence strength: moderate（観察研究ターゲットトライアルエミュレーション、適応バイアス残存可能性）
- Safety notes: ニフェジピン群で子癇・HELLP・腎不全増加あり。ラベタロール非承認国では代替薬選択に注意。
- Limitations: ラベタロール群に91%集中。未測定交絡残存可能性。RCTでない。
- Practice change potential: 高:ニフェジピン第一選択施設での変更検討トリガー
- Next action: 国内産婦人科ガイドラインとの照合、施設でのラベタロール使用状況確認
- Watch keywords: labetalol nifedipine pregnancy, 妊娠高血圧 降圧薬 安全性, target trial emulation obstetrics
- PubMed URL: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42306491
- OA URL: https://doi.org/10.1016/j.eclinm.2026.104002
- Source URLs: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/42306491
- Summary: オーストラリア7,416妊娠例のターゲットトライアルエミュレーション。ニフェジピン使用は母体複合アウトカムリスク33%増加。子癇・HELLP・腎不全増加が主因。新生児アウトカムに差なし。
- Trend summary: 妊娠高血圧の薬物治療比較研究は近年増加。ラベタロール優位のシグナルが蓄積しつつある。

- Genre: 周産期
- Rank: 3
- Score: 75
- Importance level: high
- PMID: 42307974
- DOI: 10.1177/21501319261462668
- Journal: Journal of Primary Care & Community Health
- Pub year: 2026
- Study design: システマティックレビュー・メタアナリシス

- Evidence strength: moderate（大規模SR/MA、I²=99.1%の高異質性で解釈要注意）
- Safety notes: 異質性が極めて高いためプール推定値の解釈は慎重に。地域・時期・プログラム水準による大きな差異に注意。
- Limitations: I²=99.1%と高異質性。英仏語文献のみ。出版バイアスの可能性。
- Practice change potential: 中:HIV陽性妊婦管理プログラムの地域別強化根拠

- Summary: サハラ以南アフリカ48研究のメタアナリシス。プールHIV MTCT率7.0%でWHO目標5%未達。時系列的に改善も地域差が大きい。I²=99.1%のため解釈は慎重に。
- Trend summary: PMTCTプログラム普及で母子感染率は低下傾向だが、西アフリカ等では依然高率で地域別介入が課題。
